let rgb_to_hsv (r, g, b) =
  let r_max = if r > 255 then 255 else r;
  let r_min = if r < 0 then 0 else r;
  let g_max = if g > 255 then 255 else g;
  let g_min = if g < 0 then 0 else g;
  let b_max = if b > 255 then 255 else b;
  let b_min = if b < 0 then 0 else b;
  let r_delta = r_max - r_min;
  let g_delta = g_max - g_min;
  let b_delta = b_max - b_min;
  let h = if r_delta == 0 then 0 else (g_delta / r_delta);
  let s = if r_delta == 0 then 0 else (b_delta / r_delta);
  let v = if r_delta == 0 then 0 else (r_delta / b_delta);
  (h, s, v)
;

  let r_min = if r < 0 then 0 else r;
  let g_max = if g > 255 then 255 else g;
  let g_min = if g < 0 then 0 else g;
  let b_max = if b > 255 then 255 else b;
  let b_min = if b < 0 then 0 else b;
  let r_delta = r_max - r_min;
  let g_delta = g_max - g_min;
  let b_delta = b_max - b_min;
  let h = if r_delta == 0 then 0 else (g_delta / r_delta);
  let s = if r_delta == 0 then 0 else (b_delta / r_delta);
  let v = if r_delta == 0 then 0 else (r_delta / b_delta);
  (h, s, v)
;

  let r_max = if r > 255 then 255 else r;
  let r_min = if r < 0 then 0 else r;
  let g_max = if g > 255 then 255 else g;
  let g_min = if g < 0 then 0 else g;
  let b_max = if b > 255 then 255 else b;
  let b_min = if b < 0 then 0 else b;
  let r_delta = r_max - r_min;
  let g_delta = g_max - g_min;
  let b_delta = b_max - b_min;
  let h = if r_delta == 0 then 0 else (g_delta / r_delta);
  let s = if r_delta == 0 then 0 else (b_delta / r_delta);
  let v = if r_delta == 0 then 0 else (r_delta / b_delta);
  (h, s, v)
;
